
Expand description

A trait for elements that can be styled.
Use this to opt-in to a utility CSS-like styling API.

Required Methods[](#required-methods)
--------------------------------------

[Source](../src/gpui/styled.rs.html#23)

#### fn [style](#tymethod.style)(&mut self) -> &mut [StyleRefinement](struct.StyleRefinement.html "struct gpui::StyleRefinement")

Returns a reference to the style memory of this element.

Provided Methods[](#provided-methods)
--------------------------------------

[Source](../src/gpui/styled.rs.html#19)

Dyn Compatibility[](#dyn-compatibility)
----------------------------------------

This trait is **not** [dyn compatible](https://doc.rust-lang.org/nightly/reference/items/traits.html#dyn-compatibility).

*In older versions of Rust, dyn compatibility was called "object safety", so this trait is not object safe.*
